[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m464[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m465[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m466[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m467[0m[39m:        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m468[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m469[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m470:e[0m[39mnd:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m471[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35msk_GENERAL_NAME_pop_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39msan_names, GENERAL_NAME_free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m472[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m473[0m[39m:    [0m[39mreturn TRUE;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m474[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the analysis of the heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability in [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`x509_validate_subject_aternative_names`, I will generate a fix strategy that [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maddresses all identified issues while leveraging existing, proven infrastructure in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe codebase.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability has three distinct bugs:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Bug #[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Heap Buffer Overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLines [0m[1;36m452[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m458[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m452[0m[39m allocates memory based on `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which stops at the first null byte[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m457[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m458[0m[39m copies `[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_length[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` bytes which returns the full binary [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ASN.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m strings are binary-safe and can contain embedded null bytes[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This mismatch causes: [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m-byte allocation with [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m-byte write = [0m[1;36m15[0m[39m-byte overflow[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Bug #[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Missing Null Termination [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m458[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- After `[0m[1;35mmemcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, the string lacks null termination[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mverify_san[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m893[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` which requires null termination[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This causes undefined behavior even without the overflow[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Bug #[0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Incorrect Return Value [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;36m473[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Function always returns `TRUE` regardless of validation results[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `result` variable is set to `FALSE` on validation failure but never returned[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This completely bypasses certificate validation[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Strategy - Option [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mRecommended[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Leverage Existing Infrastructure[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Approach:** Refactor `[0m[1;35mx509_validate_subject_aternative_names[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to use the proven[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mmap_subject_alt_name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mextract_string[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` infrastructure that already exists [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the codebase.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation Steps:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Modify lines [0m[1;36m433[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m474[0m[39m** in `libfreerdp/crypto/x509_utils.c`:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the manual SAN extraction and string allocation logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m440[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m468[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace with calls to `[0m[1;35mmap_subject_alt_name[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` using `[0m[1;35mextract_string[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` mapper[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Use the same pattern as `[0m[1;35mx509_utils_get_dns_names[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m561[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m598[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Specific changes:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Before lines [0m[1;36m434[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m437[0m[39m: Keep variable declarations but change types:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add: string_list list = [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep: BOOL result = TRUE;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove: char *dns_name = NULL; int i, count;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Replace lines [0m[1;36m439[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m468[0m[39m with:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;35mstring_list_initialize[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&list[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;35mmap_subject_alt_name[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcert, GEN_DNS, extract_string, &list[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Iterate through list.strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m to validate each with [0m[1;35mverify_san[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Set result = FALSE if any validation fails[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Free each string with [0m[1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Call [0m[1;35mstring_list_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&list[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Replace line [0m[1;36m473[0m[39m:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change [0m[32m"return TRUE;"[0m[39m to [0m[32m"return result;"[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory management:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Strings in `list.strings[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` are allocated by `[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mextract_string[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m297[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - These must be freed with `[0m[1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot regular `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `string_list` structure itself should be freed with `[0m[1;35mstring_list_free[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Approach Is Optimal:**[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Eliminates all three bugs simultaneously:** No strlen/length mismatch possible,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrings are properly null-terminated by OpenSSL, returns actual result[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Follows established patterns:** Uses the same infrastructure as [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mx509_utils_get_email[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m476[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m494[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `[0m[1;35mx509_utils_get_dns_names[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m561[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m598[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Reduces code duplication:** Removes ~[0m[1;36m35[0m[39m lines of buggy reimplementation[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Uses proven code:** The `[0m[1;35mextract_string[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` mapper is already used successfully [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthroughout the codebase[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Proper ASN.[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m handling:** `[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` correctly handles binary-safe [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrings [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m297[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Comment at lines [0m[1;36m575[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m576[0m[39m confirms:** After UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m conversion, there are no [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39membedded null bytes, so `[0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in `[0m[1;35mverify_san[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is safe[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Fix Strategy - Option [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mAlternative[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m: Minimal Patch[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIf refactoring is not possible, apply a minimal fix to the existing structure:[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation Steps:**[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Replace lines [0m[1;36m451[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m458[0m[39m** in `libfreerdp/crypto/x509_utils.c`:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Before line [0m[1;36m451[0m[39m: Add variable declaration:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - unsigned char* utf8_name = NULL;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Replace lines [0m[1;36m451[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m458[0m[39m:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - int length = [0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&utf8_name, gen_name->d.dNSName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       result = FALSE;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       goto end;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - dns_name = [0m[1;35mstrndup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mchar*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mutf8_name, length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mutf8_name[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdns_name == NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       result = FALSE;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       goto end;[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Replace line [0m[1;36m473[0m[39m:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change `return TRUE;` to `return result;`[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Keep lines [0m[1;36m460[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m467[0m[39m unchanged:** The validation and cleanup logic is correct[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Works:**[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mASN1_STRING_to_UTF8[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` returns the actual string length [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnot affected by [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39membedded nulls[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mstrndup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` allocates exact size + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m and null-terminates[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `[0m[1;35mOPENSSL_free[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` properly releases OpenSSL-allocated memory[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Returns the actual validation result[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Trade-offs:**[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Still has code duplication with `[0m[1;35mextract_string[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- More complex than Option [0m[1;36m1[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- But maintains existing control flow if that's required[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and Impact Analysis[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why Option [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m is Preferred:**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
